# Lang 20b Detailed Result Analysis - 2026-06-20

## 1. Report Purpose

This report records the Defects4J Lang 20b dataset validation, pre-benchmark checks, full benchmark execution, and result interpretation for the AR-QIEA true Pareto test-suite minimization protocol.

The source of truth for the protocol is `SPEC-AR-QIEA.md`. The report style follows `REPORT_EVERY_CHANGES/2026-06-16.md`.

## 7. Greedy Baseline Analysis

| Metric | Value |
|---|---:|
| MSR | 0.951297 |
| CGCC | 1.000000 |
| ETR | 0.383755 |
| CR | 1.000000 |
| Violation | 0.000000 |
| ROP | 0.756835 |
| Selected tests | 136 / 1882 |
| Total proxy execution time | 16585.007945 |
| Dominated by algorithms | `none` |

Interpretation: the greedy baseline achieves full CR and CGCC with a relatively small selected set, but it is a single deterministic coverage point rather than a Pareto front. No algorithm front point strictly dominates the greedy point under the implemented Pareto dominance rule because greedy has CGCC = 1.0 and CR = 1.0.

## 8. Pareto Front Detail

Every available feasible front point from the benchmark JSON is listed below. Selected solution bit vectors are available in the raw JSON under `cases["."].algorithms[algorithm].raw[seed_index].entries[front_point_index].solution`. They are not expanded here because each vector has 1882 bits and the raw JSON already preserves them losslessly.

## 9. ROP / Redundancy Analysis

| Algorithm | Front points | ROP mean | ROP std | ROP min | ROP max | Selected count mean | Selected count min | Selected count max | Knee MSR | Knee CGCC | Knee ETR | Knee ROP | Knee selected count |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| ar_qiea | 695 | 0.778984 | 0.008085 | 0.757466 | 0.802840 | 974.930935 | 890.000000 | 1036.000000 | 0.901006 | 0.989676 | 0.395464 | 0.757466 | 927 |
| mo_qiea | 30 | 0.788932 | 0.007006 | 0.770670 | 0.802528 | 982.266667 | 928.000000 | 1031.000000 | 0.894653 | 0.991823 | 0.375837 | 0.770670 | 989 |
| nsga2 | 527 | 0.779658 | 0.007894 | 0.763396 | 0.802600 | 960.791271 | 899.000000 | 1024.000000 | 0.885654 | 0.991045 | 0.385549 | 0.764982 | 984 |
| random_front | 820 | 0.832703 | 0.005894 | 0.814314 | 0.845088 | 1673.454878 | 1390.000000 | 1813.000000 | 0.924299 | 0.992737 | 0.233198 | 0.815394 | 1523 |

Lower ROP indicates less overlapping requirement coverage among selected tests. On this run, the strongest HV algorithm is AR-QIEA, and its ROP range is best interpreted alongside selected-count and objective trade-offs rather than as an optimized objective, because ROP is diagnostic only in the SPEC.

## 10. Statistical Analysis

| Comparison | Wilcoxon p-value | AR wins | AR losses | Ties | Result at alpha=0.05 |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| ar_qiea vs mo_qiea | 0.000000000931 | 30 | 0 | 0 | PASS |
| ar_qiea vs nsga2 | 0.000010399148 | 25 | 5 | 0 | PASS |
| ar_qiea vs random_front | 0.000000000931 | 30 | 0 | 0 | PASS |

P1 gate result: `PASS`.

The P1 gate requires `HV(ar_qiea) >= HV(mo_qiea)` and `HV(ar_qiea) >= HV(random_front)`, preferably with `p < 0.05`. Lang 20b satisfies this gate under the recorded synthetic-risk run. AR-QIEA also beats NSGA-II by mean HV with a statistically significant Wilcoxon p-value.

## 11. Detailed Interpretation

- Best mean HV: `ar_qiea` with HV mean `0.347853`.
- Largest mean Pareto front size: `random_front` with mean front size `27.333333`.
- Best maximum MSR across seeds/fronts: `random_front` with `1.000000`.
- Best maximum CGCC across seeds/fronts: `random_front` with `1.000000`.
- Best maximum ETR across seeds/fronts: `ar_qiea` with `0.398994`.

Runtime trade-off: AR-QIEA and MO-QIEA are slower than NSGA-II and random_front because they maintain and rotate a quantum-inspired population against an archive. The full benchmark runtime was about 2.81 hours on this machine. Random front is fastest per aggregate runtime but has much lower mean HV than AR-QIEA.

Paper-claim support: for this Lang 20b dataset and the current P1 synthetic risk implementation, the result supports the claim that AR-QIEA produces a higher-HV feasible Pareto front than MO-QIEA, NSGA-II, and random_front. The limitation is that mutation, centrality, and execution time are synthetic/proxy signals generated from coverage, not full real Major mutation, real Java call graph centrality, or measured test timing.

Dataset limitation: 1647 tests have zero coverage over the modified-line requirement set. This does not make the dataset invalid, but it affects interpretation because many candidate subsets can include irrelevant tests that increase selected_count and reduce ETR without improving CR/MSR/CGCC.

### Missing fields / abnormal values

- Some MO-QIEA and NSGA-II seeds produced empty feasible fronts, recorded as HV 0.0 and front_size 0.
- The full JSON is large because it stores selected solution bit vectors for every feasible front entry.

## 13. Reproduction Commands

Go to project root:

```powershell
cd "D:\FPT\Study\2026\sem5\SWT301\Quantun+Testing\OFFICIAL\quantum-testing"
```

Rerun dataset validation:

```powershell
Get-Content artifacts\pareto\lang20b_validation_20-06-2026.json
```

Rerun precheck tests:

```powershell
..\.venv\Scripts\python.exe -m pytest -q tests/test_metrics_mo.py tests/test_risk_problem.py tests/test_ar_qiea.py tests/test_nsga2.py
```

Rerun full benchmark:

```powershell
..\.venv\Scripts\python.exe scripts/pareto_benchmark.py --root datasets/defects4j/Lang/20b --seeds 42..71 --pop 40 --gens 150 --algorithms ar_qiea,mo_qiea,nsga2,random_front --risk-seed 12345 --cr-threshold 0.95 --output artifacts/pareto/lang20b_full_19-06-2026.json
```

View raw result JSON:

```powershell
Get-Content artifacts\pareto\lang20b_full_19-06-2026.json
```

View this report:

```powershell
Get-Content REPORT_EVERY_CHANGES\20B_Detail-Result-Analyst_20-06-2026.md
```
